<div id="review_671688152" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/671688152" />
    <a title="Tricia  Santos" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16453761-tricia-santos"><img alt="Tricia  Santos" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1399446032p2/16453761.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/671688152?book_show_action=true">Jul 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tricia  Santos" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tricia  Santos" href="/user/show/16453761-tricia-santos">Tricia  Santos</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16453761-tricia-santos?shelf=my-ultimate-favorites">my-ultimate-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer671688152" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10742361570200085502">First, I’d just like to say that if Alayna doesn’t want to be obsessed with Hudson Pierce, then I will gladly do all the crazy stalking for her. No, but really. Laurelin’s Fixed trilogy has a special place in my heart. Fixed On You was the book I read right after I got my iPhone stolen on vacation in Pairs three days before my birthday. I needed a distraction and Hudson Pierce was the perfect fix. It helped me feel sooo much better after crying my eyes out. It took me to a different world and I'</span>
  <span id="freeText10742361570200085502" style="display:none">First, I’d just like to say that if Alayna doesn’t want to be obsessed with Hudson Pierce, then I will gladly do all the crazy stalking for her. No, but really. Laurelin’s Fixed trilogy has a special place in my heart. Fixed On You was the book I read right after I got my iPhone stolen on vacation in Pairs three days before my birthday. I needed a distraction and Hudson Pierce was the perfect fix. It helped me feel sooo much better after crying my eyes out. It took me to a different world and I'm obsessed. It reminded me of the power of books make you forget everything else. If you haven’t read Fixed On You, you might want to do that before reading the rest of this review. And you definitely want to do that before you read Found In You. And you need to read these books immediately. How could you not want to? It’s different. It’s intense. It’s fresh. It’s captivating. It’s sexy as hell. It’s relatable on some level. It has a gorgeous, alpha male, It has a strong, quirky heroine. It makes you think. It has twists and turns. It makes you fall in love with the heroine, the hero, the plot, the writing style, and most of all, the author.<br /><br />“I’m the same man, Alayna. A man who commits to whichever plan he’s chosen. I had told myself that I couldn’t have you. So I didn’t let myself even try.”<br /><br />Found In You starts off exactly where we left off with Fixed On You. I love when books start off with a bang. Literally. Alayna has decided to give in to Hudson’s wishes and goes to spend the night with him in his apartment, where he has never brought another woman. Laurelin is magical at writing their love scenes. Hudson is dominating in the bedroom, but not in the BDSM way. Like everything she does, Alayna puts all her heart into their lovemaking.<br /><br />“Because I love you. I love you too much, like I always do, but this time I don’t regret it and I don’t wish I could take it back because you need it. So take it from me, H. Take it all from me.”<br /><br />Their chemistry is scorching and all-encompassing. Although the lingo can get pretty dirty, I get swept away in their passion. Every. Single. Time. Which is a lot. Yup, they’re at it all the time. No complaints here. So anyway, this book is mainly about Hudson and Alayna learning to be in a relationship. This is the first real time for both of them. Alayna isn’t obsessively stalking Hudson and Hudson isn’t manipulating Alayna. Alayna has already professed her love for Hudson, but Hudson isn’t able to say it.<br /><br />“Just don’t give up on us. Please, don’t give up. I’m a shell without you, Alayna. I can barely breathe when you aren’t near me, when I’m not touching you.”<br /><br />Sometimes, I forget that he hasn’t said “I love you” yet. His love for her just shines in everything he does. And he says he doesn’t know how to do romantic. Psh. I basically have two reactions to everything Hudson does: I swoon or I melt. Swooning is when he’s being sweet and doing things like buying Alayna a library. Melting is when he’s doing things like fucking Alayna EVERYWHERE. We still have a few issues from the first book, like Hudson’s awful mother, Celia being too buddy-buddy with Hudson, Alayna’s pompous brother, and Alayna’s almost affair with her boss, David. But, I loved the new issues. There were so many things I didn’t see coming. And on top of that, Alayna and Hudson talk to each other a bit about their pasts and my heart was breaking for the two of them. It was a lot more twisted that we were initially led to believe in Fixed On You I loved seeing them fight their pasts together.<br /><br />“But more importantly, if you’re in a mess of any sort, then so am I. Not legally. But because you’re mine. And I’m yours. And that means I’m tied to you in every way. Good and bad. If you can’t see that, then we have no chance.”<br /><br />Since they’re still fairly new to real relationships and to each other, they have to learn how to communicate and to share their burdens. I was proud of how they both seemed to change when they accepted that they couldn’t manage a fake relationship because everything between them was so real and intense. Alayna felt so relatable to me. She was struggling between being in love with Hudson and being obsessed with Hudson. There is a fine line separating love and lust. It’s something all girls have to deal with at one point or another. I feel like she handled it all well. Hudson can be very intense and overwhelming. That’s another thing. The book was so well written that you get sucked in to every moment, seeing and feeling everything Alayna does. Hudson was the dark, brooding man I’ve been craving lately.<br /><br />“And because I’m not skilled at expressing how I feel in words, I’m wishing I could show you exactly how into you I am at the moment.”<br /><br />Hudson has his struggles too. He internalizes it more than Alayna but he is struggling with the concept that he could deserve someone like Alayna. He has a messed up past and it holds him back at times. Alayna strips down his walls like no one else can. Usually I hate the whole “Oh, I don’t deserve you thing”, but it made sense with Alayna and Hudson. They complete each other like they never thought possible. Theirs is a story of two broken people with dark pasts learning to love and be loved. Which means that this story is not all hearts and flowers the whole time. It’s hard to figure out who you can trust in the book. Everything is just too new to them and Alayna gets pulled in every direction. I can pinpoint exactly two points where I almost threw my iPad across the room. You’ll know. I absolutely can’t wait till Forever With You. As soon as I was finished with Found In You, I was already craving more Hudson and Alayna. I loved the rollercoaster Laurelin took us on with Hudson and Alayna. Although, I’ll be extremely sad to say goodbye to them in the final installment to the Fixed trilogy, I’m ready for them to have their HEA.<br /><br />“I’m not giving up, if that’s what you’re asking. I’m so lost without you. Find me, Hudson.”<br />“I already have.”<br /><br />See full review here <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.romanceaddictbookblog.com/2013/09/review-found-in-you-by-laurelin-paige.html?zx=1bed47cedb14245">http://www.romanceaddictbookblog.com/...</a><br /><br />Ahhhh! Guess who just got an ARC?! Woohoo! Review to come closer to release date over at Romance Addict Book Blog</span>
  <a data-text-id="10742361570200085502" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_698351015" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/698351015" />
    <a title="Alyssa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/806430-alyssa"><img alt="Alyssa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393794508p2/806430.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/698351015?book_show_action=true">Aug 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alyssa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alyssa" href="/user/show/806430-alyssa">Alyssa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/806430-alyssa?shelf=rich">rich</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/806430-alyssa?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/806430-alyssa?shelf=businessman">businessman</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/806430-alyssa?shelf=dark-past">dark-past</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer698351015" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6085370103989248935"><i>** I was provided an ARC in exchange for an honest review **</i><br/><br/><b>4.5 stars</b><br/><br/>Ohhh swoon guys. Hudson is just dreamy. There was even a point in this book where I thought I hated him and I was so mad for Aleyna but... nope. Swoon.<br/><br/>I'm getting ahead of myself though.<br/><br/>This story picks up right where Fixed on You left out. As I suspected, Fixed on You really was just the beginning of Hudson and Alayna's relationship, and they still have so many things and secrets and emotions left unresolved between them. That</span>
  <span id="freeText6085370103989248935" style="display:none"><i>** I was provided an ARC in exchange for an honest review **</i><br /><br /><b>4.5 stars</b><br /><br />Ohhh swoon guys. Hudson is just dreamy. There was even a point in this book where I thought I hated him and I was so mad for Aleyna but... nope. Swoon.<br /><br />I'm getting ahead of myself though.<br /><br />This story picks up right where Fixed on You left out. As I suspected, Fixed on You really was just the beginning of Hudson and Alayna's relationship, and they still have so many things and secrets and emotions left unresolved between them. That said, I was extremely surprised when I realized just how short a span of time these books actually happen across.<br /><br />The one downside to the story is that I can't say much about what this book was about, because honestly while I was reading it the book didn't feel like it had much of a focus. This is kind of my only gripe with it. Alayna and Hudson's story and relationship develops and they face a lot of trust and communication issues that we often times don't get to read about between couples in stories because most books are about the chase and honeymoon of being together. They both need to learn to communicate, to trust one another, and to open up with one another. Sure they swapped stories in the last book about their pasts and what they did and how it has shaped the person they are... but when you really think about it we weren't actually given any details of what exactly happened and went down. We might want to say that the details don't matter, but they actually kind of do, and in this book we realize that they do.<br /><br />Hudson is still holding back on Alayna, but so is she. Despite all of Hudson's reassurances, Alayna is still scared to death and insecure about Hudson's feelings and devotion for her. She has never had a successful relationship in the past and is scared at every turn that her neurotic behavior will eventually destroy them. What was beautiful about this book was that we are pleasantly surprised to find that these fears are not just one-sided! Hudson, despite his swoony perfection, is a human being too, and he too is worried about Alayna leaving him, particularly if she finds out more details about what he actually did in his past.<br /><br />By the end of this book it takes on more purpose, but I still think it could have had more of a defined direction and plot line. I felt like the "climax" of the story was more like a subplot, yet the story itself was lacking a real clear direction.<br /><br />That said I totally enjoyed reading about Alayna and Hudson and them making their relationship work. This book really demonstrates the effort it takes. Love really isn't enough and you do honestly have to put in work to overcome pasts and fears and make relationships work.<br /><br />And Hudson. SWOON. Seriously guys. As I mentioned, there was one part towards the end where my heart just DROPPED. I was convined for PAGES that there was no recovering. That I could never forgive him. That this was a hard limit for me and I just didn't know how his actions could possibly be justified. And yet... <b>I'm okay.</b> I am still upset by Hudson but I <i>understand</i> and it makes sense and... even though the situation isn't ideal I can surprisingly deal with it and calm my heart and just really realize that people may not be perfect but that doesn't mean we have to hold it against them for that and that <i>forgiveness and understanding are key.</i><br /><br />This book is just fantastic. Knocked down half a star for the plot thing but seriously. You won't be disappointed.<br /><br />---<br /><br /><a href="http://laurelinpaige.blogspot.com/2013/08/i-have-surprise-for-you.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Read the first chapter here</a>!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer680178310" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5112974951529264288">4.5 conniving, untrusted, yet steaming stars. I LOVED this book, so why not 5 *'s...well because there is no finality at the last page. I can just feel there is a storm brewing in the calmness that was felt at conclusion. I am a fan of this series to date and this is my fave kinda plot line. Im a sucker for messed up characters and there is all kinds of crazy going on with Alayna Withers and Hudson Pierce. <br/><br/>This read picks up with Alayna and H. "together" in the real, no longer pretending. Alayna</span>
  <span id="freeText5112974951529264288" style="display:none">4.5 conniving, untrusted, yet steaming stars. I LOVED this book, so why not 5 *'s...well because there is no finality at the last page. I can just feel there is a storm brewing in the calmness that was felt at conclusion. I am a fan of this series to date and this is my fave kinda plot line. Im a sucker for messed up characters and there is all kinds of crazy going on with Alayna Withers and Hudson Pierce. <br /><br />This read picks up with Alayna and H. "together" in the real, no longer pretending. Alayna has put her heart out there and found love in Hudson whether he is willing to accept it or not. The same fears are present as Alayna is still battling her past demons in trying to not fall over the edge into obsession with Hudson, all while he is trying to actually have a relationship built on truths not manipulation. All seems well in their bubble of steamy sex and witty banter, however both of their pasts will creep back into their present and create drama for them. Can someone please slap Celia Werner or toss her over a cliff! I knew this chick was no good from the get go...Dirty B!<br /><br />I have to admit I was sucked into the read and whether the author meant to or not, I fell victim to the same insecurities Alayna felt. I am still trying to figure out if everything is a lie and if in this game of manipulation, we were all pawns. I want to believe in this couple...I want a HEA...but I am very guarded. Some people lie so beautifully that you find you are questioning your own sanity...poor Alayna! I am happy that this character has backbone and that she stays true to herself througout the read. I am also happy that Hudson seems to be "better"...i am still yearing for his declaration of Love, even though his actions are pretty clear. <br /><br />So, patiently I wait for the next book in this series...of course it is no task to have to re-read Alayna and Hudson's tale...it is quite good. It is a bit damaged, a bit psycho crazy, a bit hot, and whole lot enjoyable!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zvR7f5lAwJs2X8aZw/xq7KdaoQZrDABRFRAes8eyjk7xSg85tkcU7YPZFBObg00Xdr9Own6IX6GxHaaL4jO63A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }
